AND STOP LOSS AT ENTRY PRICE + 2.16260700 %
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

IF HIGH OF 7 BARS AGO > HIGH OF 8 BARS AGO
AND HIGH OF 8 BARS AGO > LOW OF 7 BARS AGO
AND LOW OF 7 BARS AGO > LOW OF 8 BARS AGO
AND LOW OF 8 BARS AGO > HIGH OF 2 BARS AGO
AND HIGH OF 2 BARS AGO > HIGH OF 1 BARS AGO
AND HIGH OF 1 BARS AGO > LOW OF 2 BARS AGO
AND LOW OF 2 BARS AGO > HIGH OF 0 BARS AGO
AND HIGH OF 0 BARS AGO > LOW OF 1 BARS AGO
AND LOW OF 1 BARS AGO > LOW OF 0 BARS AGO
THEN BUY NEXT BAR ON THE OPEN WITH
PROFIT TARGET AT ENTRY PRICE + 1.87352100 %
AND STOP LOSS AT ENTRY PRICE - 2.06426600 %
